country_event = {
	id = 999990
	title = "Host Nation Picked!"
	desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is now the host nation!"
	major = yes
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = "Okay"
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 999991
	title = "You are the host nation now"
	desc = "Host nation status has been transferred to you"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		UTI = {
			country_event = 999990
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = host_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Okay"
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 999992
	title = "GTFO"
	desc = "ur kicked"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = {
		name = youre_kicked_mate
		duration = -1
}
	}

	option = {
		name = "rip"
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 999993
	title = "Unsiege"
	desc = "You will be unsieged"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				controlled_by_rebels = no
			}
			change_controller = THIS
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Okay"
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 999994
	title = "Siege"
	desc = "You will siege your enemies"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					NOT = { military_access = FROM }
				}
			}
			any_owned = {
				change_controller = THIS
			}			
		}
		clr_country_flag = siege_country
	}

	option = {
		name = "Based"
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 999995
	title = "Give Sanctions Menu"
	desc = "Choose how long you want the sanctions to last for the target countries"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Nevermind"
	}
	option = {
		name = "1 Year"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { military_access = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 999996
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "2 Years"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { military_access = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 999997
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "3 Years"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { military_access = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 999998
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "4 Years"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { military_access = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 999999
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "5 Years"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { military_access = THIS }
			}
			country_event = 1000000
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 1000001
	title = "Crisies Disabled!"
	desc = "The host, $FROMCOUNTRY$, has disabled crisies!"
	major = yes
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = "Okay"
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 1000002
	title = "Host swap"
	desc = "Host's bout to swap yo ur nation"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { country_event = 1000003 }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = host_flag_tagmove
			}
			UTI = { country_event = 1000004 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = host_flag_tagmove }
			}
			UTI = { country_event = 1000005 }
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = "k"
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 1000006
	title = "Nation swap"
	desc = "Host has decided that someone's gonna swap to yo nation"
	picture = "greatpowers"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = picked_to_swap
			}
			country_event = 1000007	
			clr_country_flag = picked_to_swap
			clr_global_flag = has_chosen_swap
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = "k"
	}
}
